if (!is_file('composer.json')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: composer.json');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('composer.json')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): composer.json');
	} else if (sha1_file('composer.json') != '4798de4da0dc8b845388392987681ad297a11ac2') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): composer.json');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('composer.json', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of composer.json');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('composer.json') !== '4798de4da0dc8b845388392987681ad297a11ac2') {
		if (@sha1_file('composer.json') !== 'a4f5454df7c66751e8f5fb5310fff1aee1f09815') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: composer.json');
			$tmp = pathinfo('composer.json');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('composer.json')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('composer.json', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('composer.json') !== '4798de4da0dc8b845388392987681ad297a11ac2') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): composer.json');
		}
	}
}

	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') != 'fdde80d23182d02a0aa42bd7241eae487a6d9028') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') !== 'fdde80d23182d02a0aa42bd7241eae487a6d9028') {

			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') !== 'fdde80d23182d02a0aa42bd7241eae487a6d9028') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');

if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/functions.inc.php');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') != 'aed485d2a53d5f28273d1e68fa7230b8c0e470d8') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/functions.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/functions.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== 'aed485d2a53d5f28273d1e68fa7230b8c0e470d8') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '942481b69d7f2a78b422c87d9778ad486a0dcd5c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/functions.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/functions.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/functions.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/functions.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== 'aed485d2a53d5f28273d1e68fa7230b8c0e470d8') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/oidplus.inc.php');
	writefile_6();
	if (!is_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/oidplus.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php') != '94a95900479ca7e9e6c79f1e582f23c511cdef09') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/oidplus.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/oidplus.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php') !== '94a95900479ca7e9e6c79f1e582f23c511cdef09') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php') !== '85f93944162b4944719cd3f0cde70107ea3aa4a6') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/oidplus.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/oidplus.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/oidplus.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/oidplus.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus.inc.php') !== '94a95900479ca7e9e6c79f1e582f23c511cdef09') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/oidplus_base.js')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/oidplus_base.js');
	writefile_7();
	if (!is_file('includes/oidplus_base.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/oidplus_base.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/oidplus_base.js') != 'f2432e129a9ad6cf044d40b6c154984cb90fd75a') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus_base.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/oidplus_base.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/oidplus_base.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus_base.js') !== 'f2432e129a9ad6cf044d40b6c154984cb90fd75a') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus_base.js') !== '4c1e0452ba07d668cd0d0f3d9e9e10c7b4ebd0b2') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/oidplus_base.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/oidplus_base.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/oidplus_base.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/oidplus_base.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus_base.js') !== 'f2432e129a9ad6cf044d40b6c154984cb90fd75a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus_base.js');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): oidplus.min.js.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus.min.js.php') != '41df1676b7355fbe61e3b294d5025901e6dbc5ae') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus.min.js.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus.min.js.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of oidplus.min.js.php');
	}

	if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.js.php') !== '41df1676b7355fbe61e3b294d5025901e6dbc5ae') {
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.js.php') !== '2629eac63fafbef651ff32881e8ad54ce43000c0') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: oidplus.min.js.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('oidplus.min.js.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus.min.js.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('oidplus.min.js.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_8();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.js.php') !== '41df1676b7355fbe61e3b294d5025901e6dbc5ae') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): oidplus.min.js.php');
		}
	}
